## New Namespace Xamarin.Android.Net

### New Type Xamarin.Android.Net.AndroidClientHandler

<pre style='color: green'>
public class AndroidClientHandler : System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler, System.IDisposable {
	// constructors
	public AndroidClientHandler ();
	// properties
	public AuthenticationData PreAuthenticationData { get; set; }
	public bool ProxyAuthenticationRequested { get; }
	public System.Collections.Generic.IList&lt;AuthenticationData&gt; RequestedAuthentication { get; }
	public bool RequestNeedsAuthorization { get; }
	public System.Collections.Generic.IList&lt;Java.Security.Cert.Certificate&gt; TrustedCerts { get; set; }
	// methods
	protected void AssertSelf ();
	protected virtual Javax.Net.Ssl.KeyManagerFactory ConfigureKeyManagerFactory (Java.Security.KeyStore keyStore);
	protected virtual Java.Security.KeyStore ConfigureKeyStore (Java.Security.KeyStore keyStore);
	protected virtual Javax.Net.Ssl.TrustManagerFactory ConfigureTrustManagerFactory (Java.Security.KeyStore keyStore);
	protected override void Dispose (bool disposing);
	protected override System.Threading.Tasks.Task&lt;System.Net.Http.HttpResponseMessage&gt; SendAsync (System.Net.Http.HttpRequestMessage request, System.Threading.CancellationToken cancellationToken);
	protected virtual void SetupRequest (System.Net.Http.HttpRequestMessage request, Java.Net.HttpURLConnection conn);
}
</pre>

public class AuthenticationData {
	// constructors
	public AuthenticationData ();
	// properties
	public IAndroidAuthenticationModule AuthModule { get; set; }
	public string Challenge { get; }
	public AuthenticationScheme Scheme { get; set; }
	public bool UseProxyAuthentication { get; set; }
}

### New Type Xamarin.Android.Net.AuthenticationScheme

<pre style='color: green'>
[Serializable]
public enum AuthenticationScheme {
	Basic = 2,
	Digest = 3,
	None = 0,
	Unsupported = 1,
}
</pre>

### New Type Xamarin.Android.Net.IAndroidAuthenticationModule

<pre style='color: green'>
public interface IAndroidAuthenticationModule {
	// properties
	public virtual string AuthenticationType { get; }
	public virtual bool CanPreAuthenticate { get; }
	public virtual AuthenticationScheme Scheme { get; }
	// methods
	public virtual System.Net.Authorization Authenticate (string challenge, Java.Net.HttpURLConnection request, System.Net.ICredentials credentials);
	public virtual System.Net.Authorization PreAuthenticate (Java.Net.HttpURLConnection request, System.Net.ICredentials credentials);
}
</pre>
